    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Active], [p].[Code], [p].[CreatedTime], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Photo], [p].[ProductBrandId], [p].[Search], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [p0].[Name] AS [Name0], [p2].[Id] AS [Id2], [p2].[Name] AS [Name2]
    FROM [Product] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [ProductCategory] AS [p0] ON [p].[ProductCategoryId] = [p0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [ProductBrand] AS [p1] ON [p].[ProductBrandId] = [p1].[Id]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Id0] AS [ProductCategoryId], [t].[Name0] AS [ProductCategoryName], [t].[Name], [t].[Code], [t].[Description], [t].[Photo], [t].[Active], [t].[CreatedTime], [t].[Id2] AS [ProvinceId], [t].[Name2] AS [ProvinceName], [t].[Search], [p3].[Name] AS [ProductBrandName]

    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Active], [p].[Code], [p].[CreatedTime], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Photo], [p].[ProductBrandId], [p].[Search], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [p0].[Name] AS [Name0], [p2].[Id] AS [Id2], [p2].[Name] AS [Name2]
    FROM [Product] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [ProductCategory] AS [p0] ON [p].[ProductCategoryId] = [p0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [ProductBrand] AS [p1] ON [p].[ProductBrandId] = [p1].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Province] AS [p2] ON [p].[ProvinceId] = [p2].[Id]
    WHERE ((([p].[Active] = 1) AND ([p0].[Active] = 1)) AND ([p1].[Active] = 1)) AND ([p2].[Active] = 1)
    ORDER BY [p].[Name] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [ProductBrand] AS [p3] ON [t].[ProductBrandId] = [p3].[Id]
ORDER BY [t].[Name] DESC
